<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 1.01 Entry into a Material 
Definitive Agreement.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As previously disclosed on August&nbsp;8, 
2016, Emerge Energy Services LP (the &#147;Partnership&#148;) entered into a 
Securities Purchase Agreement (the &#147;Purchase Agreement&#148;) with an 
institutional investor (the &#147;Purchaser&#148;) to issue and sell to the 
Purchaser in a private placement (the &#147;Private Placement&#148;) an 
aggregate principal amount of $20 million of the Partnership&#146;s 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units (the &#147;Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units&#148;)
and a warrant (the &#147;Warrant&#148;) that may be exercised to purchase common
units representing limited partner interests in the Partnership (&#147;Common 
Units&#148;).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In connection with the closing of the 
Private Placement on August&nbsp;15, 2016, the Partnership issued to the 
Purchaser the Warrant to purchase approximately 890,000 Common Units at an 
exercise price of $10.82 per Common Unit. The issuance of the Warrant pursuant 
to the Purchase Agreement is being made in reliance upon an exemption from the 
registration requirements of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended (the 
&#147;Securities Act&#148;), pursuant to Section&nbsp;4(a)
(2)&nbsp;thereof.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In addition, pursuant to the Purchase 
Agreement, on August&nbsp;15, 2016, the Partnership and the Purchaser entered 
into a registration rights agreement (the &#147;Registration Rights 
Agreement&#148;), pursuant to which the Partnership provided the Purchaser with 
certain demand and piggyback registration rights to register the Conversion 
Shares (as defined below) and Common Units issuable upon exercise of the 
Warrant, subject to penalties and other customary provisions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The descriptions of the Warrant and the 
Registration Rights Agreement contained in this Item 1.01 are qualified in their
entirety by reference to the full text of the Warrant and the Registration 
Rights Agreement, which are filed as Exhibits 10.1 and 10.2 hereto, 
respectively, and are incorporated by reference herein. The information 
regarding the Warrant and the Registration Rights Agreement under Item 1.01 of 
the Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K filed on August&nbsp;8, 2016 is incorporated
by reference into this Item 1.01.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">2<a name="PB_2_011627_141"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade 
align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='2',FILE='C:\JMS\108736\16-16835-1\task8068477\16835-1-

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 3.03 Material Modification to 
Rights of Security Holders.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:28.6pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The terms of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Units, and the Common Units issuable upon conversion of the Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units, are set forth in Amendment No.&nbsp;1 to the First Amended and 
Restated Agreement of Limited Partnership of the Partnership, dated 
August&nbsp;15, 2016 (the &#147;Partnership Agreement Amendment&#148;). As 
described in the Partnership Agreement Amendment, the Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Units entitle the holders of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units to certain rights
that are senior to the rights of holders of Common Units, such as distribution 
rights or rights upon liquidation of the Partnership. In the event of any
liquidation, dissolution and winding up of the Partnership or a sale, exchange 
or other disposition of all or substantially all of the assets of the 
Partnership, either voluntary or involuntary, the holders of the Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units shall be entitled to receive a distribution of the assets of the
Partnership, in an amount up to the positive value of such holder&#146;s capital
account, prior and in preference to any distribution of any assets of the 
Partnership to the holders of the Common Units.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:28.6pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information regarding the Series&nbsp;A
Preferred Units set forth in Items 1.01 and 5.03 hereof is incorporated by 
reference into this Item 3.03.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 5.03 Amendments to Articles of 
Incorporation or Bylaws; Change in Fiscal Year.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On and effective as of August&nbsp;15, 
2016, Emerge Energy Services GP LLC, the general partner of the Partnership (the
&#147;General Partner&#148;), executed the Partnership Agreement Amendment for 
the purpose of authorizing the issuance of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units and
the Common Units issuable upon conversion of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Units.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to the Partnership Agreement 
Amendment, holders of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units receive no distributions
except as payable on the underlying Common Units on an as-converted basis at the
time of such distribution. The Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units, subject to the 
satisfaction of customary equity conditions, will automatically convert into 
Common Units (the &#147;Conversion Shares&#148;) in two tranches (each, an 
&#147;Automatic Conversion Date&#148;) as follows: (a)&nbsp;50% of the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units shall automatically convert into Common Units on 
the tenth trading day following the earlier of (i)&nbsp;the Registration Date 
(as defined in the Partnership Agreement Amendment) and (ii)&nbsp;the date that 
all of the Conversion Shares can be sold pursuant to Rule&nbsp;144 (the 
&#147;Initial Conversion Date&#148;), and (b)&nbsp;the remaining 50% of the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units shall automatically convert into Common Units on 
the tenth trading day following the date ninety (90) days after the Initial 
Conversion Date. On each applicable Automatic Conversion Date, the Conversion 
Price of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units shall be equal to the lower of 
(i)&nbsp;the Initial Conversion Price and (ii)&nbsp;90% of the Market Price (as 
defined in the Partnership Agreement Amendment) on the applicable Automatic 
Conversion Date.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units rank 
senior to the Common Units with respect to the payment of distributions and 
distribution of assets upon liquidation, dissolution and winding up, in each 
case, as described in Item 3.03 hereof. The Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units have 
no stated maturity and are not subject to mandatory redemption or any sinking 
fund and will remain outstanding indefinitely unless redeemed by the Partnership
or converted into Common Units at the election of the Partnership or the 
Preferred Unit Holders or in connection with a Change of Control (as defined in 
the Partnership Agreement Amendment).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units vote as a
separate class on any matter on which unitholders are entitled to vote that 
adversely affects the rights, powers, privileges or preferences of the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units or</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">3<a name="PB_3_011628_7608"></a></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">as required by law. The consent of a majority of the 
then-outstanding Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units shall be required to approve any 
matter for which the Preferred Unit Holders are entitled to vote as a separate 
class.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The description of the Partnership 
Agreement Amendment contained in this Item 5.03 is qualified in its entirety by 
reference to the full text of the Partnership Agreement Amendment, which is 
filed as Exhibit&nbsp;3.1 hereto and is incorporated by reference herein. The 
information regarding the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units set forth in Items 1.01 
and 3.03 hereof is incorporated by reference into this Item 5.03.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 7.01 Regulation FD 
Disclosure.</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:28.6pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On August&nbsp;16, 2016, the Partnership 
issued a press release announcing the closing of the Private Placement. A copy 
of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:23.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information contained in this Item 
7.01, including Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 attached hereto, is being furnished to the 
Securities and Exchange Commission and shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for
the purpose of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as 
amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;). In addition, none of such information 
shall be incorporated by reference in any filing made by EMES under the Exchange
Act or the Securities Act except to the extent specifically referenced in any 
such filings.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font

LP</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Amendment No.&nbsp;1 (this 
&#147;<i>Amendment</i>&#148;) to the First Amended and Restated Agreement of 
Limited Partnership of Emerge Energy Services LP, a Delaware limited partnership
(the &#147;<i>Partnership</i>&#148;), dated as of May&nbsp;14, 2013 (as so 
amended, the &#147;<i>Partnership Agreement</i>&#148;), is entered into 
effective as of August&nbsp;15, 2016 at the direction of Emerge Energy Services 
GP LLC, as the general partner of the Partnership (the &#147;<i>General 
Partner</i>&#148;), pursuant to authority granted to it in Section&nbsp;13.1 of 
the Partnership Agreement.&#160; Capitalized terms used but not defined herein 
have the meanings ascribed to them in the Partnership Agreement.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">RECITALS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Section&nbsp;5.4(a)&nbsp;of the Partnership 
Agreement provides that the Partnership may issue additional Partnership 
Interests for any Partnership purpose at any time and from time to time to such 
Persons and for such consideration and on such terms and conditions as shall be 
established by the General Partner in its sole discretion, all without the 
approval of any Limited Partners;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Section&nbsp;5.4(b)&nbsp;of the Partnership 
Agreement provides that the Partnership Interests authorized to be issued by the
Partnership pursuant to Section&nbsp;5.4(a)&nbsp;may be issued in one or more 
classes, or one or more series of any such classes, with such designations, 
preferences, rights, powers and duties (which may be senior to existing classes 
and series of Partnership Interests) as shall be fixed by the General Partner in
the exercise of its sole discretion;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, Section&nbsp;13.1(g)&nbsp;of the Partnership 
Agreement provides that the General Partner, without the approval of any Limited
Partners, may amend any provision of the Partnership Agreement that, in the 
discretion of the General Partner, is necessary or advisable in connection with 
the creation, authorization or issuance of any class or series of Partnership 
Interests pursuant to Section&nbsp;5.4 of the Partnership Agreement; and</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
weight:bold;">WHEREAS</font></b>, the General Partner deems it advisable and in 
the best interest of the Partnership to effect this Amendment to provide for 
(i)&nbsp;the creation of a new class of Units to be designated as Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units and to fix the preferences and the relative participating, 
optional and other special rights, powers and duties pertaining to the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units, including, without limitation, the conversion of 
the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units into Common Units in accordance with the terms
described herein, (ii)&nbsp;the issuance of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units to
the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchaser pursuant to the Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Purchase Agreement and (iii)&nbsp;such other matters as are provided herein.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">NOW, 
THEREFORE</font></b>, in consideration of the covenants, conditions and 
agreements contained herein, the General Partner does hereby amend the 
Partnership Agreement as follows:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.</font><font size="1" style="font-

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1

</font><u>Amendment</u>.&#160; The Partnership Agreement is hereby amended as 
follows:</p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Black Scholes Consideration 
Value</i>&#148; means the value of the applicable Option, Convertible Security 
or Adjustment Right (as the case may be) as of the date of issuance thereof 
calculated using the Black Scholes Option Pricing Model obtained from the 
&#147;OV&#148; function on Bloomberg utilizing (i)&nbsp;an underlying price per 
Unit equal to the Closing Sale Price of the Common Units on the Trading Day 
immediately preceding the public announcement of the execution of definitive 
documents with respect to the issuance of such Option, Convertible Security or 
Adjustment Right (as the case may be), (ii)&nbsp;a risk-free interest rate 
corresponding to the U.S. Treasury rate for a period equal to the remaining term
of such Option, Convertible Security or Adjustment Right (as the case may be) as
of the date of issuance of such Option, Convertible Security or Adjustment Right
(as the case may be), (iii)&nbsp;a zero cost of borrow and (iv)&nbsp;an expected
volatility equal to the greater of 100% and the 30 day volatility obtained from 
the HVT function on Bloomberg (determined utilizing a 365-day annualization 
factor) as of the Trading Day immediately following the date of issuance of such
Option, Convertible Security or Adjustment Right (as the case may 
be).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Closing Bid Price</i>&#148; and 
&#147;<i>Closing Sale Price</i>&#148; means, for any security as of any date, 
the last closing bid price and last closing trade price, respectively, for such 
security on the Principal Market, as reported by Bloomberg, or, if the Principal
Market begins to operate on an extended hours basis and does not designate the 
closing bid price or the closing trade price (as the case may be) then the last 
bid price or last trade price, respectively, of such security prior to 4:00:00 
p.m., New York time, as reported by Bloomberg, or, if the Principal Market is 
not the principal securities exchange or trading market for such security, the 
last closing bid price or last trade price, respectively, of such security on 
the principal securities exchange or trading market where such security is 
listed or traded as reported by Bloomberg, or if the foregoing do not apply, the
last closing bid price or last trade price, respectively, of such security in 
the over-the-counter market on the electronic bulletin Board of Directors for 
such security as reported by Bloomberg, or, if no closing bid price or last 
trade price, respectively, is reported for such security by Bloomberg, the 
average of the bid prices, or the ask prices, respectively, of any market makers
for such security as reported in the &#147;pink sheets&#148; by OTC Markets 
Group Inc. (formerly Pink Sheets LLC). If the Closing Bid Price or the Closing 
Sale Price cannot be calculated for a security on a particular date on any of 
the foregoing bases, the Closing Bid Price or the Closing Sale Price (as the 
case may be) of such security on such date shall be the fair market value as 
mutually determined by the Partnership and the Required Holder. If the 
Partnership and the Required Holders are unable to agree upon the fair market 
value of such security, then such dispute shall be resolved in accordance with 
the procedures in <u>Section</u></font></p>

Units to be issued in connection with the event requiring determination (or

requiring this determination (without regards to any limitations on conversion

regulations of the Eligible Market on which the Common Units are then listed or 
designated for quotation (as applicable); (vi)&nbsp;on each day during the 
Equity Conditions Measuring Period, no public announcement of a pending,
proposed or intended Fundamental Transaction shall have occurred which has not 
been abandoned, terminated or consummated; (vii)&nbsp;the Partnership shall have
no knowledge of any fact that would reasonably be expected to cause (1)&nbsp;any
Registration Statement required to be filed pursuant to the Registration Rights 
Agreement to not be effective or the prospectus contained therein to not be 
available for the resale of the applicable Required Minimum Securities Amount of
Registrable Securities in accordance with the terms of the Registration Rights 
Agreement or (2)&nbsp;any Registrable Securities to not be eligible for sale

Units and exercise of the Warrants) and no Current Information Failure exists or

have been in compliance with each, and shall not have breached any

or warranties subject to material adverse effect or materiality, which may not 
be breached in any respect) or materially breached any covenant or other term or
condition of any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Transaction Document, including,

and there shall not exist a Triggering Event or an event that with the passage

that (A)&nbsp;all such issuances (taking into account the Common Units issuable

Units issued and Outstanding immediately prior to the Subscription Date and 
(B)&nbsp;the exercise price of any such options is not lowered, none of such 
options are amended to increase the number of Units issuable thereunder and none
of the terms or conditions of any such options are otherwise materially changed 
in any manner that adversely affects any of the Buyers; (ii)&nbsp;Common Units 
issued upon the conversion or exercise of Convertible Securities (other than 
standard options to purchase Common Units issued pursuant to the LTIP that are 
covered by clause (i)&nbsp;above) issued prior to the Subscription Date;<i> 
provided</i> that the conversion price of any such Convertible Securities (other
than standard options to purchase Common Units issued pursuant to the LTIP that 
are covered by clause (i)&nbsp;above) is not lowered, none of such Convertible 
Securities (other than standard options to purchase Common Units issued pursuant
to the LTIP that are covered by clause (i)&nbsp;above) are amended to increase 
the number of units issuable thereunder and none of the terms or conditions of 
any such Convertible Securities (other than standard options to purchase Common 
Units issued pursuant to the LTIP that are covered by clause (i)&nbsp;above) are
otherwise materially changed in any manner that adversely affects any of the 
Buyers; (iii)&nbsp;the Common Units issuable upon conversion of the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units or otherwise pursuant to the terms of this 
Amendment; <i>provided</i> that the terms of this Amendment are not amended, 
modified or changed on or after the Subscription Date (other than anti-dilution 
adjustments pursuant to the terms thereof in effect as of the Subscription Date)
and (iv)&nbsp;the Common Units issuable upon exercise of the Warrants; 
<i>provided</i> that the terms of the Warrant are not amended, modified or 
changed on or after the Subscription Date (other than anti-dilution adjustments 
pursuant to the terms thereof in effect as of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Closing Date).</font></p>

means (A)&nbsp;that the Partnership shall, directly or indirectly, including 
through subsidiaries, Affiliates or otherwise, in one or more related 
transactions, (i)&nbsp;consolidate or merge with or into (whether or not the 
Partnership is the surviving corporation) another Subject Entity, or 
(ii)&nbsp;sell, assign, transfer, convey or otherwise dispose of all or 
substantially all of the properties or assets of the Partnership or any of its 
&#147;significant subsidiaries&#148; (as defined in Rule&nbsp;1-02 of Regulation
S-X) to one or more Subject Entities, or (iii)&nbsp;make, or allow one or more 
Subject Entities to make, or allow the Partnership to be subject to or have its 
Common Units be subject to or party to one or more Subject Entities making, a 
purchase, tender or exchange offer that is accepted by the holders of at least 
66-2/3% of the Outstanding Units, or (iv)&nbsp;consummate a unit or stock or 
share purchase agreement or other business combination (including, without 
limitation, a reorganization, recapitalization, spin-off or scheme of 
arrangement) with one or more Subject Entities whereby all such Subject 
Entities, individually or in the aggregate, acquire at least 66-2/3% of the
Outstanding Units (including Units held by the General Partner and its 
Affiliates) voting as a single class, or (v)&nbsp;reorganize, recapitalize or 
reclassify its Common Units whereby one or more Subject Entities, individually 
or in the aggregate, acquire at least 66-2/3% of the Outstanding Units, 
(B)&nbsp;that the Partnership shall, directly or indirectly, including through 
subsidiaries, Affiliates or otherwise, in one or more related transactions, 
allow any Subject Entity individually or the Subject Entities in the aggregate 
to be or become the &#147;beneficial owner&#148; (as defined in Rule&nbsp;13d-3

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">the 1934 Act), directly or indirectly, whether through
acquisition, purchase, assignment, conveyance, tender, tender offer, exchange, 
reduction in Outstanding Common Units, merger, consolidation, business 
combination, reorganization, recapitalization, spin-off, scheme of arrangement, 
reorganization, recapitalization or reclassification or otherwise in any manner 
whatsoever, of either (x)&nbsp;at least 50% of the aggregate ordinary voting 
power represented by issued and Outstanding Common Units, (y)&nbsp;at least 50% 
of the aggregate ordinary voting power represented by issued and Outstanding 
Common Units not held by all such Subject Entities as of the date of this 
Warrant calculated as if any Common Units held by all such Subject Entities were
not Outstanding, or (z)&nbsp;a percentage of the aggregate ordinary voting power
represented by issued and Outstanding Common Units or other equity securities of
the Partnership sufficient to allow such Subject Entities to effect a statutory 
short form merger or other transaction requiring other Unitholders of the 
Partnership to surrender their Common Units without approval of the Unitholders 
of the Partnership or (C)&nbsp;directly or indirectly, including through 
subsidiaries, Affiliates or otherwise, in one or more related transactions, the 
issuance of or the entering into any other instrument or transaction structured 
in a manner to circumvent, or that circumvents, the intent of this definition in
which case this definition shall be construed and implemented in a manner 
otherwise than in strict conformity with the terms of this definition to the 
extent necessary to correct this definition or any portion of this definition 
which may be defective or inconsistent with the intended treatment of such 
instrument or transaction.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>General Partner</i>&#148; has the 
meaning given to such term in the introductory paragraph.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Judgment Conversion Date</i>&#148;
has the meaning given to such term in <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(r)(i)
(B)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Judgment Currency</i>&#148; has 
the meaning given to such term in <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(r)(i)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Liquidation Preference</i>&#148; 
means, with respect to each Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit, the sum of the Stated 
Value plus all accrued and unpaid distributions on such Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Unit to the date of dissolution of the Partnership.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Market Price</i>&#148; means, as 
of any time of determination, the lower of (i)&nbsp;the VWAP of the Common Units
on the Trading Day ended immediately preceding the time of determination, and 
(ii)&nbsp;the quotient of (x)&nbsp;the sum of the VWAP of the Common Units on 
each of the ten (10)&nbsp;consecutive Trading Days ending and including the 
Trading Day ended immediately preceding the time of determination, 
<i>divided</i> by (y)&nbsp;ten (10).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Maximum Percentage</i>&#148; has 
the meaning given to such term in <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iv)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>New Issuance Price</i>&#148; has 
the meaning given to such term in <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Noncompensatory Option</i>&#148; 
has the meaning set forth in Treasury Regulation Section&nbsp;1.721-
2(f).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Notice Failure</i>&#148; has the 
meaning given to such term in <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iii)(B)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Options</i>&#148; means any 
rights, warrants or options to subscribe for or purchase Common Units or 
Convertible Securities.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Parent Entity</i>&#148; of a 
Person means an entity that, directly or indirectly, controls the applicable 
Person and whose common stock or equivalent equity security is quoted or listed 
on an Eligible Market, or, if there is more than one such Person or Parent 
Entity, the Person or Parent Entity with the largest public market 
capitalization as of the date of consummation of the Fundamental 
Transaction.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Date.&#160; All such determinations to be 
appropriately adjusted for any Unit splits, Unit distributions, Unit 
combinations or other similar transaction during such measuring 
period.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Triggering Event Period 
Termination Date</i>&#148; has the meaning given to such term in 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(v)(A)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Triggering Events</i>&#148; means 
each of the following events:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the failure of the initial 
Registration Statement required to be filed pursuant to the Registration Rights 
Agreement (as defined in the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase Agreement) to be 
declared effective by the Commission on or prior to the 180th day after the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Closing Date and the Partnership does not meet the 
current public information requirements under Rule&nbsp;144 in respect of the 
Registrable Securities (as defined under the Registration Rights Agreement);</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>if, during the 
Effectiveness Period (as defined in the Registration Rights Agreement), the 
effectiveness of a Registration Statement registering Registrable Securities 
lapses for more than an aggregate of 60 calendar days (which need not be 
consecutive calendar days) during any 12-month period, or the Holders shall not 
otherwise be permitted to resell Registrable Securities under the Registration 
Statement for more than an aggregate of 60 calendar days (which need not be 
consecutive calendar days) during any 12-month period;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the suspension from 
trading or failure of the Common Units to be trading or listed (as applicable) 
on an Eligible Market for a period of five (5)&nbsp;consecutive Trading 
Days;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the Partnership&#146;s 
notice, written or oral, to any holder of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units or 
Warrants, including, without limitation, by way of public announcement or 
through any of its agents, at any time, of its intention not to comply, as 
required, with a request for exercise of any Warrants for Warrant Units in 
accordance with the provisions of the Warrants or a request for conversion of 
any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units into Common Units that is requested in 
accordance with the provisions of this Amendment, in each case other than
pursuant to <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iv)</u>, <u>Section&nbsp;6.4(b)</u>&nbsp;or 
<u>Section&nbsp;6.5</u>;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the 
Partnership&#146;s failure to pay to any Holder any amount when and as due under
this Amendment (including, without limitation, the Partnership&#146;s failure to
pay any redemption payments or amounts hereunder), the Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Purchase Agreement or any other Series&nbsp;A Preferred Transaction Document or 
any other agreement, document, certificate or other instrument delivered in 
connection with the transactions contemplated hereby and thereby (in each case, 
whether or not permitted pursuant to the Delaware Act), except, in the case of a
failure to pay distributions when and as due, in each such case only if such 
failure remains uncured for a period of at least three (3)&nbsp;Trading 
Days;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the 
Partnership, on two or more occasions, either (A)&nbsp;fails to cure a 
Conversion Failure or a Delivery Failure (as defined in the Warrants) by 
delivery of the required number of Common Units within five (5)&nbsp;Trading 
Days after the applicable Conversion Date or Exercise Date (as defined in the 
Warrants) (as the case may be) or (B)&nbsp;fails to remove any restrictive 
legend on any certificate or any Common Units issued to such Holder upon 
conversion or exercise (as the case may be) of any Securities (as defined in the
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase Agreement) acquired by such Holder under the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase Agreement as and when required by such 
Securities or the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase Agreement, unless 
otherwise</p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

final judgment or judgments for the payment of money aggregating in excess of 
$10,000,000 are rendered against the Partnership and/or any of its Subsidiaries 
and which judgments are not, within thirty (30) days after the entry thereof, 
bonded, discharged, settled or stayed pending appeal, or are not discharged 
within thirty (30) days after the expiration of such stay; <i>provided</i>, 
<i>however</i>, any judgment which is covered by insurance or an indemnity from 
a credit worthy party shall not be included in calculating the $10,000,000 
amount set forth above so long as the Partnership provides each Holder a written
statement from such insurer or indemnity provider (which written statement shall
be reasonably satisfactory to each Holder) to the effect that such judgment is 
covered by insurance or an indemnity and the Partnership or such Subsidiary (as 
the case may be) will receive the proceeds of such insurance or indemnity within
thirty (30) days of the issuance of such judgment;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>U.S. Dollars</i>&#148; has the 
meaning given to such term in <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(q)(ii)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Valuation Event</i>&#148; has the 
meaning given to such term in <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)(D)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Variable Price</i>&#148; has the 
meaning given to such term in <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(iii)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Variable Price 
Securities</i>&#148; has the meaning given to such term in 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(iii)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>VWAP</i>&#148; means, for any 
security as of any date, the dollar volume-weighted average price for such 
security on the Principal Market (or, if the Principal Market is not the 
principal trading market for such security, then on the principal securities 
exchange or securities market on which such security is then traded) during the 
period beginning at 9:30:01 a.m., New York time, and ending at 4:00:00 p.m., New
York time, as reported by Bloomberg through its &#147;Volume at Price&#148; 
function or, if the foregoing does not apply, the dollar volume-weighted average
price of such security in the over-the-counter market on the electronic bulletin
Board of Directors for such security during the period beginning at 9:30:01 
a.m., New York time, and ending at 4:00:00 p.m., New York time, as reported by 
Bloomberg, or, if no dollar volume-weighted average price is reported for such 
security by Bloomberg for such hours, the average of the highest closing bid 
price and the lowest closing ask price of any of the market makers for such 
security as reported in the &#147;pink sheets&#148; by OTC Markets Group Inc. 
(formerly Pink Sheets LLC). If the VWAP cannot be calculated for such security 
on such date on any of the foregoing bases, the VWAP of such security on such 
date shall be the fair market value as mutually determined by the Partnership 
and the Required Holders. All such determinations shall be appropriately 
adjusted for any Unit distribution, Unit split, Unit combination, 
recapitalization or other similar transaction during such period.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Warrants</i>&#148; has the meaning
ascribed to such term in the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase Agreement, and 
shall include all warrants issued in exchange therefor or replacement 
thereof.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Warrant Units</i>&#148; means, 
collectively, the Common Units issuable upon exercise of the 
Warrants.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Warrant Uniformity 
Failure</i>&#148; has the meaning given to such term in 
<u>Section&nbsp;6.5</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<i>Warrant Uniformity Failure 
Unit</i>&#148; has the meaning given to such term in 
<u>Section&nbsp;6.5</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font>Section&nbsp;5.3(a)&nbsp;is hereby amended and restated as follows:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Partnership shall 
maintain for each Partner (or a beneficial owner of Partnership Interests held 
by a nominee in any case in which the nominee has furnished the identity of such
owner to the Partnership in accordance with Section&nbsp;6031(c)&nbsp;of the 
Code or any other method acceptable to the General Partner) owning a Partnership
Interest a separate Capital Account with respect to such Partnership Interest in
accordance with the rules&nbsp;of Treasury Regulation Section&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)
(iv).&#160; For the avoidance of doubt, (i)&nbsp;the conversion feature of each 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit shall be treated as a Noncompensatory Option, and 
each Record Holder of a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit shall be treated as a 
partner in the Partnership for federal income tax purposes and (ii)&nbsp;each 
Warrant shall be treated as a Noncompensatory Option but shall not be treated as
exercised upon issuance, and, therefore, each Record Holder of a Warrant shall 
not be treated as a partner in the Partnership for federal income tax purposes 
until such Record Holder exercises such Warrant and receives a Warrant 
Unit.&#160; The initial Capital Account attributable to the Common Units to be 
issued to the Underwriters pursuant to <u>Section&nbsp;5.1(d)</u>&nbsp;shall 
equal the product of the number of Common Units so issued to the Underwriters 
and the Initial Unit Price for each such Common Unit (and the initial Capital 
Account balance attributable to each such Common Unit shall equal its Initial 
Unit Price).&#160; The initial Capital Account balance in respect of each 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit issued on the applicable date shall be the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit Price for such</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">13<a name="PB_13_072854_7091"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade 
align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='13',FILE='C:\JMS\108183\16-16835-1\task8067174\16835-1-ke-

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit. The Capital Account 
balance of each holder of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units in respect of its 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units shall not be increased or decreased except as 
otherwise provided in this Agreement.&#160; Thereafter, such Capital Account 
shall be increased by (i)&nbsp;the amount of all Capital Contributions made to 
the Partnership with respect to such Partnership Interest pursuant to this 
Agreement and (ii)&nbsp;all items of Partnership income and gain (including 
income and gain exempt from tax) computed in accordance with 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.3(b)</u>&nbsp;and allocated with respect to such Partnership 
Interest pursuant to <u>Section&nbsp;6.1</u>, and decreased by (x)&nbsp;the 
amount of cash or Net Agreed Value of all actual and deemed distributions of 
cash or property made with respect to such Partnership Interest and (y)&nbsp;all
items of Partnership deduction and loss computed in accordance with 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.3(b)</u>&nbsp;and allocated with respect to such Partnership 
Interest pursuant to <u>Section&nbsp;6.1</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" 
style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font>Section&nbsp;5.3(d)(i)&nbsp;is hereby amended and restated as 
follows:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>(i)&nbsp;In accordance with
Treasury Regulation Section&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(f), on an issuance of 
additional Partnership Interests for cash or Contributed Property, the issuance 
of a Noncompensatory Option, the issuance of Partnership Interests as 
consideration for the provision of services or the conversion of the General 
Partner&#146;s (and its Affiliates&#146;) Combined Interest to Common Units 
pursuant to Section&nbsp;11.3(b), the Capital Account of each Partner and the 
Carrying Value of each Partnership property immediately prior to such issuance 
shall be adjusted upward or downward to reflect any Unrealized Gain or 
Unrealized Loss attributable to such Partnership property, and any such 
Unrealized Gain or Unrealized Loss shall be treated, for purposes of maintaining
Capital Accounts, as if it had been recognized on an actual sale of each such 
property for an amount equal to its fair market value immediately prior to such 
issuance and had been allocated among the Partners at such time pursuant to 
Section&nbsp;6.1 in the same manner as any item of gain or loss actually 
recognized during such period would have been allocated; <i>provided, 
however,</i> that in the event of the issuance of a Partnership Interest 
pursuant to the exercise of a Noncompensatory Option where the right to share in
Partnership capital represented by such Partnership Interest differs from the 
consideration paid to acquire and exercise such option, the Carrying Value of 
each Partnership property immediately after the issuance of such Partnership 
Interest shall be adjusted upward or downward to reflect any Unrealized Gain or 
Unrealized Loss attributable to such Partnership property and the Capital 
Accounts of the Partners shall be adjusted in a manner consistent with Treasury 
Regulation Section&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(s);<i> provided further</i>, 
<i>however</i>, that in the event of an issuance of Partnership Interests for a 
de minimis amount of cash or Contributed Property, in the event of an issuance 
of a Noncompensatory Option to acquire a <i>de minimis</i> Partnership Interest,
or in the event of an issuance of a de minimis amount of Partnership Interests 
as consideration for the provision of services, the General Partner may 
determine that such adjustments are unnecessary for the proper administration of
the Partnership.&#160; If, upon the occurrence of an event described in this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.3(d)</u>, a Noncompensatory Option of the Partnership is 
outstanding, the Partnership shall adjust the Carrying Value of each Partnership
property in accordance with Treasury Regulation Sections 1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(f)
(1)&nbsp;and 1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(h)(2).&#160; In determining such Unrealized Gain 
or Unrealized Loss, the aggregate fair market value of all Partnership property 
(including cash or cash equivalents) immediately prior to the issuance of 
additional Partnership Interests (or, in the case of an event described in this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.3(d)</u>&nbsp;resulting from the exercise of a Noncompensatory
Option, immediately after the issuance of the Partnership Interest acquired 
pursuant to the exercise of such Noncompensatory Option if required pursuant to 
Treasury Regulation Section&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(s)(1)) shall be determined by
the General Partner using such method of valuation as it may adopt.&#160; In
making its determination of the fair market values of individual properties, the
General Partner may determine that it is appropriate to first determine an 
aggregate value for the Partnership, based on the current trading price of the 
Common Units, taking fully into account the fair market value of the Partnership
Interests of all Partners at such time, and then allocate such aggregate value 
among the individual properties of the Partnership (in such manner as it 
determines is appropriate).</p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font>Article&nbsp;V is hereby amended to add a new Section&nbsp;5.8 creating a
new series of Units as follows:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Section&nbsp;5.8&#160; <i>Establishment of 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units</i></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>General</i>.&#160; The 
General Partner hereby designates and creates a series of Units to be designated
as &#147;Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units&#148; having the terms and conditions set
forth herein.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Conversion of 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units</i>. At any time after the Series&nbsp;A Preferred
Closing Date, each Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit shall be convertible into 
validly issued, fully paid and non-assessable Common Units (as defined below), 
on the terms and conditions set forth in this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)</u>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font><i>Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s Conversion Right</i>. Subject to
the provisions of <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iv)</u>, at any time or times on or 
after the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Closing Date, each Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder shall be entitled to convert any portion of the Outstanding Series&nbsp;A
Preferred Units held by such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder into Common Units at
the Conversion Rate.&#160; The Partnership shall not issue any fraction of a 
Common Unit upon any conversion.&#160; If the issuance would result in the 
issuance of a fraction of a Common Unit, the Partnership shall round such 
fraction of a Common Unit up to the nearest whole Unit. The Partnership shall 
pay any and all transfer, stamp, issuance and similar taxes, costs and expenses 
(including, without limitation, fees and expenses of the Transfer Agent) that 
may be payable with respect to the issuance and delivery of Common Units upon 
conversion of any Conversion Amount.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Conversion 
Rate</i>.&#160; The number of Common Units issuable upon conversion of any 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit pursuant to <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)
(i)</u>&nbsp;shall be determined by dividing (x)&nbsp;the Conversion Amount of 
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit by (y)&nbsp;the Conversion Price (the 
&#147;<i>Conversion Rate</i>&#148;):</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font>&#147;<i>Conversion Amount</i>&#148; means, with respect to each 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit, as of the applicable date of determination, the 
sum of (1)&nbsp;the Stated Value thereof plus (2)&nbsp;the Additional Amount 
thereon as of such date of determination.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font>&#147;<i>Conversion Price</i>&#148; means, with respect to each 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit, as of any Conversion Date or other date of 
determination, $10.15.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Mechanics of Conversion</i>.&#160; 
The conversion of each Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit shall be conducted in the 
following manner:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A)</font><font
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Optional 
Conversion</i>.&#160; To convert a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit into Common 
Units on any Conversion Date, a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder shall deliver 
(whether via facsimile, electronic mail or otherwise), for receipt on or prior 
to 11:59 p.m., New York time, on such date, a copy of an executed notice of 
conversion of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units subject to such conversion in 
the form attached hereto as <u>Exhibit&nbsp;B</u> (the &#147;<i>Conversion 
Notice</i>&#148;) to the Partnership. If required by <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(l)
(iii)</u>, within three (3)&nbsp;Trading Days following a conversion of any such
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units as aforesaid, such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder 
shall surrender to a nationally recognized overnight delivery service for 
delivery to the Partnership the original certificates representing the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units (the &#147;S<i>eries&nbsp;A Preferred Unit 
Certificates</i>&#148;) so</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">15<a name="PB_15_073002_4141"></a></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">converted as aforesaid (or an indemnification 
undertaking with respect to the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units in the case of its
loss, theft or destruction as contemplated by <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(l)
(ii)</u>).&#160; On or before the first (1st) Trading Day following the date of 
receipt of a Conversion Notice, the Partnership shall transmit by facsimile or 
electronic mail an acknowledgment of confirmation, in the form attached hereto 
as <u>Exhibit&nbsp;C</u>, of receipt of such Conversion Notice to such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder and the Transfer Agent, which confirmation shall 
constitute an instruction to the Transfer Agent to process such Conversion 
Notice in accordance with the terms herein. On or before the third (3rd) Trading
Day following the date of receipt of a Conversion Notice (or such earlier date 
as required pursuant to the 1934 Act or other applicable law, rule&nbsp;or 
regulation for the settlement of a trade initiated on the applicable Conversion 
Date of such Common Units issuable pursuant to such Conversion Notice) (the 
&#147;<i>Unit Delivery Deadline</i>&#148;), the Partnership shall 
(1)&nbsp;provided that the Transfer Agent is participating in DTC&#146;s Fast 
Automated Securities Transfer Program, credit such aggregate number of Common 
Units to which such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder shall be entitled to such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s or its designee&#146;s balance account 
with DTC through its Deposit/Withdrawal at Custodian system, or (2)&nbsp;if the 
Transfer Agent is not participating in the DTC Fast Automated Securities 
Transfer Program, issue and deliver (via reputable overnight courier) to the 
address as specified in such Conversion Notice, a certificate, registered in the
name of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder or its designee, for the number of 
Common Units to which such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder shall be entitled. If 
the number of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units represented by the Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Unit Certificate(s)&nbsp;submitted for conversion pursuant to 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(l)(iii)</u>&nbsp;is greater than the number of Series&nbsp;A
Preferred Units being converted, then the Partnership shall, as soon as 
practicable and in no event later than three (3)&nbsp;Trading Days after receipt
of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit Certificate(s)&nbsp;and at its own expense, 
issue and deliver to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder (or its designee) a new
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit Certificate (in accordance with 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(l)(iv)</u>) representing the number of Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units not converted.&#160; The Person or Persons entitled to receive 
the Common Units issuable upon a conversion of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units 
shall be treated for all purposes as the record holder or holders of such Common
Units on the Conversion Date.&#160; Notwithstanding anything to the contrary 
contained in this Amendment or the Registration Rights Agreement, after the 
effective date of the Registration Statement (as defined in the Registration 
Rights Agreement) and prior to any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s receipt
of the notice of a Grace Period (as defined in the Registration Rights 
Agreement), the Partnership shall cause the Transfer Agent to deliver unlegended
Common Units to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder (or its designee) in 
connection with any sale of Registrable Securities (as defined in the 
Registration Rights Agreement) with respect to which such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder has entered into a contract for sale, and delivered a copy of 
the prospectus included as part of the particular Registration Statement to the 
extent applicable, and for which such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder has not yet
settled.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font><i>Partnership&#146;s Failure to Timely Convert</i>.&#160; If the 
Partnership shall fail, for any reason or for no reason, on or prior to the 
applicable Unit Delivery Deadline, either (I)&nbsp;if the Transfer Agent is not 
participating in the DTC Fast Automated Securities Transfer Program, to issue 
and deliver to a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder (or its designee) a certificate 
for the number of Common Units</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

align:center;">16<a name="PB_16_073022_8627"></a></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">to which such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder is 
entitled and register such Common Units on the Partnership&#146;s Unit register 
or, if the Transfer Agent is participating in the DTC Fast Automated Securities 
Transfer Program, to credit the balance account of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder or such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s designee with DTC for such 
number of Common Units to which such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder is entitled 
upon such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s conversion of Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units (as the case may be) or (II)&nbsp;if the Registration Statement 
covering the resale of the Common Units that are the subject of the Conversion 
Notice (the &#147;<i>Unavailable Conversion Units</i>&#148;) is not available 
for the resale of such Unavailable Conversion Units and the Partnership fails to
promptly, but in no event later than as required pursuant to the Registration 
Rights Agreement (x)&nbsp;so notify such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder and 
(y)&nbsp;deliver the Common Units electronically without any restrictive legend 
by crediting such aggregate number of Common Units to which such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder is entitled pursuant to such exercise to such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder&#146;s or its designee&#146;s balance account with DTC through
its Deposit/Withdrawal At Custodian system (the event described in the 
immediately foregoing clause (II)&nbsp;is hereinafter referred as a 
&#147;<i>Notice Failure</i>&#148; and together with the event described in 
clause (I)&nbsp;above, a &#147;<i>Conversion Failure</i>&#148;), and if on or 
after such Unit Delivery Deadline such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder purchases 
(in an open market transaction or otherwise) Common Units to deliver in 
satisfaction of a sale by such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder of all or any 
portion of the number of Common Units issuable upon such conversion that such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder so is entitled to receive from the Partnership, 
then, in addition to all other remedies available to such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder, the Partnership shall, within three (3)&nbsp;Business Days 
after receipt of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s request and in such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s discretion, either: (I)&nbsp;pay cash to 
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder in an amount equal to such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder&#146;s total purchase price (including brokerage commissions 
and other out-of-pocket expenses, if any) for the Common Units so purchased 
(including, without limitation, by any other Person in respect, or on behalf, of
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder) (the &#147;<i>Buy-In Price</i>&#148;), at 
which point the Partnership&#146;s obligation to so issue and deliver such 
certificate or credit such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s balance account
with DTC for the number of Common Units to which such Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder is entitled upon such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s conversion 
hereunder (as the case may be) (and to issue such Common Units) shall terminate,
or (II)&nbsp;promptly honor its obligation to so issue and deliver to such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder a certificate or certificates representing such 
Common Units or credit such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s balance 
account with DTC for the number of Common Units to which such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder is entitled upon such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s 
conversion hereunder (as the case may be) and pay cash to such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder in an amount equal to the excess (if any) of the Buy-In Price 
over the product of (x)&nbsp;such number of Common Units multiplied by 
(y)&nbsp;the lowest Closing Sale Price of the Common Units on any Trading Day 
during the period commencing on the date of the applicable Conversion Notice and
ending on the date of such issuance and payment under this clause 
(II).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Pro Rata 
Conversion; Disputes</i>. In the event that the Partnership receives a 
Conversion Notice from more than one Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder for the same
Conversion Date and the Partnership can convert some, but not all, of</p>
