<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units submitted for 
conversion, the Partnership shall convert from each Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder electing to have Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units converted on such date a
pro rata amount of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units submitted for conversion on such date based on the number of 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units submitted for conversion on such date by such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder relative to the aggregate number of Series&nbsp;A
Preferred Units submitted for conversion on such date. In the event of a dispute
as to the number of Common Units issuable to a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder in
connection with a conversion of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units, the Partnership 
shall issue to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder the number of Common Units 
not in dispute and resolve such dispute in accordance with 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(p)</u>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Limitation on Beneficial Ownership</i>. 
The Partnership shall not effect the conversion of any of the Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units held by a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder, and such Series&nbsp;A
Preferred Holder shall not have the right to convert any of the Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units held by such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder pursuant to the 
terms and conditions of this Amendment and any such conversion shall be null and
void and treated as if never made, to the extent that after giving effect to 
such conversion, such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder together with the other 
Attribution Parties collectively would beneficially own in excess of 4.99% (the 
&#147;<i>Maximum Percentage</i>&#148;) of the Common Units Outstanding 
immediately after giving effect to such conversion.&#160; For purposes of the 
foregoing sentence, the aggregate number of Common Units beneficially owned by 
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder and the other Attribution Parties shall 
include the number of Common Units held by such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder 
and all other Attribution Parties plus the number of Common Units issuable upon 
conversion of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units with respect to which the 
determination of such sentence is being made, but shall exclude Common Units 
which would be issuable upon (A)&nbsp;conversion of the remaining, nonconverted 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units beneficially owned by such Series&nbsp;A Preferred
Holder or any of the other Attribution Parties and (B)&nbsp;exercise or 
conversion of the unexercised or nonconverted portion of any other securities of
the Partnership (including, without limitation, any convertible notes, 
convertible preferred Units or warrants, including the Warrants) beneficially 
owned by such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder or any other Attribution Party 
subject to a limitation on conversion or exercise analogous to the limitation 
contained in this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iv)</u>.&#160; For purposes of this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iv)</u>, beneficial ownership shall be calculated in 
accordance with Section&nbsp;13(d)&nbsp;of the 1934 Act.&#160; For purposes of 
determining the number of Outstanding Common Units a Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder may acquire upon the conversion of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units 
without exceeding the Maximum Percentage, such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder 
may rely on the number of Outstanding Common Units as reflected in (x)&nbsp;the 
Partnership&#146;s most recent Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K, Quarterly Report
on Form&nbsp;10-Q, Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K or other public filing with 
the SEC, as the case may be, (y)&nbsp;a more recent public announcement by the 
Partnership or (z)&nbsp;any other written notice by the Partnership or the 
Transfer Agent, if any, setting forth the number of Common Units Outstanding 
(the &#147;<i>Reported Outstanding Unit Number</i>&#148;).&#160; If the 
Partnership receives a Conversion Notice from a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder 
at a time when the actual number of Outstanding Common Units is less than the 
Reported Outstanding Unit Number, the Partnership shall notify such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder in writing of the number of Common Units then 
Outstanding and, to the extent that such Conversion Notice would otherwise cause
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s beneficial ownership, as determined 
pursuant to this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iv)</u>, to exceed the Maximum 
Percentage, such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder must notify the Partnership of a
reduced number of Common Units to be purchased pursuant to</p>

power to vote or to transfer the Excess Units. Upon delivery of a written notice
to the Partnership, any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder may from time to time 
increase (with such increase not effective until the sixty-first (61st) day 
after delivery of such notice) or decrease the Maximum Percentage of such

specified in such notice; <i>provided</i> that (i)&nbsp;any such increase in the
Maximum Percentage will not be effective until the sixty-first (61st) day after 
such notice is delivered to the Partnership and (ii)&nbsp;any such increase or 
decrease will apply only to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder and the other 
Attribution Parties and not to any other Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder.&#160; 
For purposes of clarity, the Common Units issuable to a Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder pursuant to the terms of this Amendment in excess of the Maximum 
Percentage shall not be deemed to be beneficially owned by such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder for any purpose including for purposes of 
Section&nbsp;13(d)&nbsp;or Rule&nbsp;16a-1(a)(1)&nbsp;of the 1934 Act.&#160; No 
prior inability to convert such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units pursuant to this 
paragraph shall have any effect on the applicability of the provisions of this 
paragraph with respect to any subsequent determination of convertibility. The 
provisions of this paragraph shall be construed and implemented in a manner 
otherwise than in strict conformity with the terms of this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iv)</u>&nbsp;to the extent necessary to correct this 
paragraph (or any portion of this paragraph) which may be defective or

<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iv)</u>&nbsp;or to make changes or supplements necessary

holder of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

</font><i>General</i>.&#160; Subject to <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iv)</u>, on each 
of (x)&nbsp;the tenth (10th) Trading Day after the Registration Date (the 
&#147;<i>First Automatic Conversion Date</i>&#148;) and (y)&nbsp;the tenth 
(10th) Trading Day after the ninetieth (90th) calendar day after the First 
Automatic Conversion Date (the &#147;<i>Second Automatic Conversion 
Date</i>&#148; and, together with the First Automatic Conversion Date, each an 
&#147;<i>Automatic Conversion Date</i>&#148;), so long as no Triggering Event 
has occurred and is continuing (unless waived by the applicable Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder) and no Equity Conditions Failure then exists, 50% of the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units initially purchased by such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder (as adjusted downward on a Unit-by-Unit basis for any 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units converted</p>

nonassessable Common Units at a conversion price equal to the lower of 
(x)&nbsp;the Conversion Price then in effect and (y)&nbsp;90% of the Market

adjusted downward only to the applicable Automatic Conversion Price.</font></p>

(iv)</u>&nbsp;(such number of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units resulting in the

Units shall be adjusted downward only to the applicable Automatic Conversion 
Price.&#160; For the avoidance of doubt, at any time on or after such Automatic 
Conversion Date, such Blocked Units may be converted into Blocked Conversion 
Units at such Automatic Conversion Price, in whole or in part, by the delivery 
of a Conversion Notice pursuant to the mechanics set forth in 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(iii)</u>&nbsp;(with such &#147;Automatic Conversion

</font><i>Automatic Redemption upon Bankruptcy Triggering Event</i>.&#160; 
Notwithstanding anything to the contrary herein, and notwithstanding any 
conversion that is then required or in process, upon any Bankruptcy Triggering 
Event, whether occurring prior to or following an Automatic Conversion Date, the
Partnership shall immediately redeem, in cash, each of the Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units then Outstanding at a redemption price (the &#147;<i>Bankruptcy 
Redemption Price</i>&#148;) equal to the greater of (i)&nbsp;the product of 
(A)&nbsp;the Conversion Amount to be redeemed multiplied by (B)&nbsp;the 
Redemption Premium and (ii)&nbsp;the product of (X)&nbsp;the Conversion Rate 
then in effect with respect to the Conversion Amount multiplied by (Y)&nbsp;the 
product of (1)&nbsp;the Redemption Premium multiplied by (2)&nbsp;the greatest 
Closing Sale Price of the Common Units on any Trading Day during the period 
commencing on the date immediately preceding such Bankruptcy Triggering Event 
and ending on the date the Partnership makes the entire payment required to
be</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">made under this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(g)</u>, without 
the requirement for any notice or demand or other action by any Series&nbsp;A

Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder may, in its sole discretion, waive such right to

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Change of Control 
Redemption Right</i>. No sooner than twenty (20) Trading Days nor later than ten
(10)&nbsp;Trading Days prior to the consummation of a Change of Control (the 
&#147;<i>Change of Control Date</i>&#148;), but not prior to the public 
announcement of such Change of Control, the Partnership shall deliver written 
notice thereof via facsimile and overnight courier to each Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder (a &#147;<i>Change of Control Notice</i>&#148;). At any time 
during the period beginning after a Holder&#146;s receipt of a Change of Control
Notice or such Holder becoming aware of a Change of Control if a Change of 
Control Notice is not delivered to such Holder in accordance with the 
immediately preceding sentence (as applicable) and ending on the later of twenty
(20) Trading Days after (A)&nbsp;consummation of such Change of Control or 
(B)&nbsp;the date of receipt of such Change of Control Notice, such Holder may 
require the Partnership to redeem all or any portion of such Holder&#146;s 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units by delivering written notice thereof 
(&#147;<i>Change of Control Redemption Notice</i>&#148;) to the Partnership, 
which Change of Control Redemption Notice shall indicate the number of 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units such Holder is electing to have the Partnership 
redeem. Each Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit subject to redemption pursuant to this
<u>Section 5.8(g)(ii)</u>&nbsp;shall be redeemed by the Partnership in cash at a
price equal to the greatest of (i)&nbsp;the product of (w)&nbsp;the Change of 
Control Redemption Premium multiplied by (y)&nbsp;the Conversion Amount being 
redeemed, (ii)&nbsp;the product of (x)&nbsp;the Change of Control Redemption 
Premium multiplied by (y)&nbsp;the product of (A)&nbsp;the Conversion Amount 
being redeemed multiplied by (B)&nbsp;the quotient determined by dividing 
(I)&nbsp;the greatest Closing Sale Price of the Common Units during the period 
beginning on the date immediately preceding the earlier to occur of (1)&nbsp;the
consummation of the applicable Change of Control and (2)&nbsp;the public 
announcement of such Change of Control and ending on the date such Series&nbsp;A
Preferred Holder delivers the Change of Control Redemption Notice by 
(II)&nbsp;the Conversion Price then in effect and (iii)&nbsp;the product of
(y)&nbsp;the Change of Control Redemption Premium multiplied by (z)&nbsp;the 
product of (A)&nbsp;the Conversion Amount being redeemed multiplied by 
(B)&nbsp;the quotient of (I)&nbsp;the aggregate cash consideration and the 
aggregate cash value of any non-cash consideration per Common Unit to be paid to
such holders of the Common Units upon consummation of such Change of Control 
(any such non-cash consideration constituting publicly-traded securities shall 
be valued at the highest of the Closing Sale Price of such securities as of the 
Trading Day immediately prior to the consummation of such Change of Control, the
Closing Sale Price of such securities on the Trading Day immediately following 
the public announcement of such proposed Change of Control and the Closing Sale 
Price of such securities on the Trading Day immediately prior to the public 
announcement of such proposed Change of Control) divided by (II)&nbsp;the 
Conversion Price then in effect (the &#147;<i>Change of Control Redemption 
Price</i>&#148;). Redemptions required by this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(g)
(ii)</u>&nbsp;shall have priority to payments to all other Unitholders of the 
Partnership in connection with such Change of Control. To the extent redemptions
required by this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(g)(ii)</u>&nbsp;are deemed or determined by
a court of competent jurisdiction to be prepayments of the Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units by the Partnership, such redemptions shall be deemed to be 
voluntary prepayments. Notwithstanding anything to</p>

Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder. Accordingly, any redemption premium due under 
this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(g)(ii)</u>&nbsp;is intended by the parties to be, and

The Partnership shall make payment of the applicable Change of Control

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1

Control if such notice is received prior to the consummation of such Change of 
Control and within five (5)&nbsp;Business Days after the Partnership&#146;s 
receipt of such notice otherwise.&#160; Notwithstanding anything herein to the 
contrary, in connection with any redemption hereunder at a time a Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder is entitled to receive a cash payment under any of the other 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Transaction Documents, at the option of such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder delivered in writing to the Partnership, the 
applicable Redemption Price hereunder shall be increased by the amount of such 
cash payment owed to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder under such other 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Transaction Document and, upon payment in full or 
conversion in accordance herewith, shall satisfy the Partnership&#146;s payment 
obligation under such other Series&nbsp;A Preferred Transaction Document.&#160; 
In the event of a redemption of less than all of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Units, the Partnership shall promptly cause to be issued and delivered to such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder a new Preferred Certificate (in accordance with 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(l)</u>) representing the number of Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Units which have not been redeemed. In the event that the Partnership does not 
pay the applicable Redemption Price to a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder within 
the time period required for any reason (including, without limitation, to the 
extent such payment is prohibited pursuant to the Delaware Act), at any time 
thereafter and until the Partnership pays such unpaid Redemption Price in full, 
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder shall have the option, in lieu of 
redemption, to require the Partnership to promptly return to such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder all or any of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units that were 
submitted for redemption and for which the applicable Redemption Price has not 
been paid.&#160; Upon the Partnership&#146;s receipt of such notice, 
(x)&nbsp;the applicable Redemption Notice shall be null and void with respect to
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units, and (y)&nbsp;the Partnership shall 
immediately return the applicable Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit Certificate, or 
issue a new Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit Certificate (in accordance with 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(l)(iv)</u>), to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder, and in 
each case the Additional Amount of such Series&nbsp;A</p>

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Redemption by Multiple Holders</i>.&#160; 
Upon the Partnership&#146;s receipt of a Redemption Notice from any 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder for redemption or repayment as a result of an 
event or occurrence substantially similar to the events or occurrences described
in this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(g)(iv)</u>, the Partnership shall immediately, but 
no later than one (1)&nbsp;Business Day of its receipt thereof, forward to each 
other Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder by facsimile or electronic mail a copy of 
such notice. If the Partnership receives one or more Redemption Notices, during 
the seven (7)&nbsp;Business Day period beginning on and including the date which
is three (3)&nbsp;Business Days prior to the Partnership&#146;s receipt of the 
initial Redemption Notice and ending on and including the date which is three 
(3)&nbsp;Business Days after the Partnership&#146;s receipt of the initial 
Redemption Notice and the Partnership is unable to redeem all principal, 
interest and other amounts designated in such initial Redemption Notice and such
other Redemption Notices received during such seven (7)&nbsp;Business Day 
period, then the Partnership shall redeem a pro rata amount from each 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder based on the principal amount of the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units submitted for redemption pursuant to such 
Redemption Notices received by the Partnership during such seven 
(7)&nbsp;Business Day period.</p>

</font><i>Purchase Rights</i>. In addition to any adjustments pursuant to 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)</u>&nbsp;below, if at any time the Partnership grants, 
issues or sells any Options, Convertible Securities or rights to purchase Units,
warrants, securities or other property pro rata to all or substantially all of 
the record holders of any class of Common Units (the &#147;<i>Purchase 
Rights</i>&#148;), then each Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder will be entitled to 
acquire, upon the terms applicable to such Purchase Rights, the aggregate 
Purchase Rights which such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder could have acquired if
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder had held the number of Common Units 
acquirable upon complete conversion of all the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units 
(without taking into account any limitations or restrictions on the 
convertibility of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units) held by such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder immediately prior to the date on which a record is taken for 
the grant, issuance or sale of such Purchase Rights, or, if no such record is 
taken, the date as of which the record holders of Common Units are to be 
determined for the grant, issue or sale of such Purchase Rights (provided, 
however, to the extent that such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s right to 
participate in any such Purchase Right would result in such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder and the other Attribution Parties exceeding the Maximum 
Percentage, then such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder shall not be entitled to 
participate in such Purchase Right to the extent of the Maximum Percentage (and 
shall not be entitled to beneficial ownership of such Common Units as a result 
of such Purchase Right (and beneficial ownership) to the extent of any such
excess) and such Purchase Right to such extent shall be held in abeyance for 
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder until such time or times, if ever, as its 
right thereto would not result in such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder and the 
other Attribution Parties exceeding the Maximum Percentage), at which time or 
times such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder shall be granted such right (and any 
Purchase Right granted, issued or sold on such initial Purchase Right or on any 
subsequent Purchase Right to be held similarly in abeyance) to the same extent 
as if there had been no such limitation.</p>

(ii)</u>&nbsp;shall not be duplicative of other payments made under another this

the New Issuance Price. For all purposes of the foregoing (including, without

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Option for such price per Unit. For purposes of this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)(A)</u>, the lowest price per Unit for which one Common
Unit is issuable upon the exercise of any such Option or upon conversion, 
exercise or exchange of any Convertible Securities issuable upon exercise of any
such Option or otherwise pursuant to the terms thereof shall be equal to 
(1)&nbsp;the lower of (x)&nbsp;the sum of the lowest amounts of consideration
(if any) received or receivable by the Partnership with respect to any one 
Common Unit upon the granting or sale of such Option, upon exercise of such

issuable upon exercise of such Option or otherwise pursuant to the terms thereof
and (y)&nbsp;the lowest exercise price set forth in such Option for which one

conversion, exercise or exchange of any Convertible Securities issuable upon 
exercise of any such Option or otherwise pursuant to the terms thereof minus 
(2)&nbsp;the sum of all amounts paid or payable to the holder of such Option (or
any other Person) upon the granting or sale of such Option, upon exercise of 
such Option and upon conversion, exercise or exchange of any Convertible 
Security issuable upon exercise of such Option or otherwise pursuant to the 
terms thereof plus the value of any other consideration received or receivable 
by, or benefit conferred on, the holder of such Option (or any other Person). 
Except as contemplated below, no further adjustment of the Conversion Price 
shall be made upon the actual issuance of such Common Unit or of such 
Convertible Securities upon the exercise of such Options or otherwise pursuant 
to the terms thereof or upon the actual issuance of such Common Unit upon 
conversion, exercise or exchange of such Convertible Securities.</font></p>

such Common Unit shall be deemed to be Outstanding and to have been issued and

(i)(B)</u>, the &#147;lowest price per Unit for which one Common Unit is

Convertible Security or otherwise pursuant to the terms thereof and (y)&nbsp;the

paid or payable to the holder of such Convertible Security (or any other Person)
upon the issuance or sale of such Convertible Security plus the value of any 
other consideration received or receivable by, or benefit conferred on, the 
holder of such Convertible Security (or any other Person). Except as

upon the actual issuance of such Common Unit upon conversion, exercise or

upon exercise of any Options for which adjustment of the Conversion Price has

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Change in 
Option Price or Rate of Conversion</i>. If the purchase or exercise price 
provided for in any Options, the additional consideration, if any, payable upon 
the issue, conversion, exercise or exchange of any Convertible Securities, or 
the rate at which any Convertible Securities are convertible into or exercisable
or exchangeable for Common Units increases or decreases at any time, the 
Conversion Price in effect at the time of such increase or decrease shall be 
adjusted to the Conversion Price which would have been in effect at such time 
had such Options or Convertible Securities provided for such increased or 
decreased purchase price, additional consideration or increased or decreased 
conversion rate (as the case may be) at the time initially granted, issued or 
sold. For purposes of this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)(C)</u>, if the terms of any
Option or Convertible Security that was Outstanding as of the Subscription Date 
are increased or decreased in the manner described in the immediately preceding 
sentence, then such Option or Convertible Security and the Common Units deemed 
issuable upon exercise, conversion or exchange thereof shall be deemed to have 
been issued as of the date of such increase or decrease. No adjustment pursuant 
to this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)(C)</u>&nbsp;shall be made if such adjustment 
would result in an increase of the Conversion Price then in effect.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">D)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Calculation 
of Consideration Received</i>. If any Option and/or Convertible Security and/or 
Adjustment Right is issued in connection with the issuance or sale or deemed 
issuance or sale of any other securities of the Partnership (as determined by 
the Required Holders, the &#147;<i>Primary Security</i>,&#148; and such Option 
and/or Convertible Security and/or Adjustment Right, the &#147;<i>Secondary 
Securities</i>&#148;), together comprising one integrated transaction (or one or
more transactions if such issuances or sales or deemed issuances or sales of 
securities of the Partnership either (A)&nbsp;have at least one investor or 
purchaser in common, (B)&nbsp;are consummated in reasonable proximity to each 
other and/or (C)&nbsp;are consummated under the same plan of financing), the 
consideration per Common Unit with respect to such Primary Security shall be 
deemed to be equal to the difference of (x)&nbsp;the lowest price per Unit for 
which one Common Unit was issued in such integrated transaction (or was deemed 
to be issued pursuant to <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)(A)</u>&nbsp;or 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)(B)</u>&nbsp;above, as applicable) solely with respect 
to such Primary Security, minus (y)&nbsp;with respect to such Secondary 
Securities, the sum of (A)&nbsp;the Black Scholes Consideration Value of each 
such Option, if any, (B)&nbsp;the fair market value (as determined by the 
Required Holders in good faith) or the Black Scholes Consideration Value, as 
applicable, of such Adjustment Right, if any, and (C)&nbsp;the fair market value
(as determined by the Required Holder) of such Convertible Security, if any, in 
each case, as determined on a per Unit basis in accordance with this
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)(D)</u>.&#160; If any Common Units, Options or 
Convertible Securities are issued or sold or deemed to have been issued or sold 
for cash, the consideration received therefor (for the purpose of determining 
the consideration paid for such Common Units, Option or Convertible Security, 
but not for the purpose of the calculation of the Black Scholes Consideration 
Value) will be deemed to be the net amount of consideration received by the 
Partnership therefor. If any Common Units, Options or Convertible Securities are
issued or sold for a consideration other than cash (for the purpose of 
determining the consideration paid for such Common</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Units, Option or Convertible Security, but not for the
purpose of the calculation of the Black Scholes Consideration Value), the amount
of such consideration received by the Partnership will be the fair value of such
consideration, except where such consideration consists of publicly traded 
securities, in which case the amount of consideration received by the 
Partnership for such securities will be the average VWAP of such security for 
the five (5)&nbsp;Trading Day period immediately preceding the date of receipt. 
If any Common Units, Options or Convertible Securities are issued to the owners 
of the non-surviving entity in connection with any merger in which the 
Partnership is the surviving entity (for the purpose of determining the 
consideration paid for such Common Units, Option or Convertible Security, but 
not for the purpose of the calculation of the Black Scholes Consideration 
Value), the amount of consideration therefor will be deemed to be the fair value
of such portion of the net assets and business of the non-surviving entity as is
attributable to such Common Units, Options or Convertible Securities (as the 
case may be). The fair value of any consideration other than cash or publicly 
traded securities will be determined jointly by the Partnership and the Required
Holders. If such parties are unable to reach agreement within ten (10)&nbsp;days
after the occurrence of an event requiring valuation (the &#147;<i>Valuation 
Event</i>&#148;), the fair value of such consideration will be determined within
five (5)&nbsp;Trading Days after the tenth (10th) day following such Valuation 
Event by an independent, reputable appraiser jointly selected by the Partnership
and the Required Holders. The determination of such appraiser shall be final and
binding upon all parties absent manifest error and the fees and expenses of such
appraiser shall be borne by the Partnership.</font></p>

Date</i>. If the Partnership takes a record of the holders of Common Units for 
the purpose of entitling them (A)&nbsp;to receive a distribution payable in 
Common Units, Options or in Convertible Securities or (B)&nbsp;to subscribe for 
or purchase Common Units, Options or Convertible Securities, then such record 
date will be deemed to be the date of the issue or sale of the Common Units 
deemed to have been issued or sold upon the making of such distribution or the
date of the granting of such right of subscription or purchase (as the case may 
be).</p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Adjustment of 
Conversion Price upon Subdivision or Combination of Common Units</i>. Without 
limiting any provision of <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(f)</u>&nbsp;or 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)</u>, but excluding any distributions made to the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holders pursuant to <u>Section&nbsp;6.3(a)</u>, if the 
Partnership at any time on or after the Subscription Date subdivides (by any 
Unit split, Unit distribution, Unit combination, recapitalization or other 
similar transaction)&#160; one or more classes of its Outstanding Common Units 
into a greater number of Units, the Conversion Price in effect immediately prior
to such subdivision will be proportionately reduced. Without limiting any 
provision of <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(f)</u>&nbsp;or <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)</u>, 
if the Partnership at any time on or after the Subscription Date combines (by 
any Unit split, Unit distribution, Unit combination, recapitalization or other 
similar transaction) one or more classes of its Outstanding Common Units into a 
smaller number of Units, the Conversion Price in effect immediately prior to 
such combination will be proportionately increased. Any adjustment pursuant to 
this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(ii)</u>&nbsp;shall become effective immediately 
after the effective date of such subdivision or combination. If any event 
requiring an adjustment under this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(ii)</u>&nbsp;occurs 
during the period that a Conversion Price is calculated hereunder, then the 
calculation of such Conversion Price shall be adjusted appropriately to reflect 
such event.</p>

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1

Section&nbsp;4(n)&nbsp;of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase Agreement, if the
Partnership in any manner issues or sells or enters into any agreement to issue

securities, &#147;<i>Variable Price Securities</i>&#148;) that are issuable 
pursuant to such agreement or convertible into or exchangeable or exercisable 
for Common Units pursuant to such Options or Convertible Securities, as 
applicable, at a price which varies or may vary with the market price of the 
Common Units, including by way of one or more reset(s)&nbsp;to a fixed price, 
but exclusive of such formulations reflecting customary anti-dilution provisions
(such as Unit splits, Unit combinations, Unit distributions and similar 
transactions) (each of the formulations for such variable price being herein
referred to as, the &#147;<i>Variable Price</i>&#148;), the Partnership shall 
provide written notice thereof via facsimile or electronic mail and overnight 
courier to each Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder on the date of such agreement 
and/or the issuance of such Common Units, Convertible Securities or Options, as 
applicable.&#160; From and after the date the Partnership enters into such 
agreement or issues any such Variable Price Securities, each Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder shall have the right, but not the obligation, in its sole 
discretion to substitute the Variable Price for the Conversion Price upon 
conversion of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units by designating in the Conversion
Notice delivered upon any conversion of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units that 
solely for purposes of such conversion such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder is 
relying on the Variable Price rather than the Conversion Price then in 
effect.&#160; A Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s election to rely on a 
Variable Price for a particular conversion of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units 
shall not obligate such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder to rely on a Variable 
Price for any future conversions of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iv)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Other Events</i>. In the event that the 
Partnership (or any Subsidiary) shall take any action to which the provisions 
hereof are not strictly applicable, or, if applicable, would not operate to 
protect any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder from dilution or if any event occurs 
of the type contemplated by the provisions of this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)</u>&nbsp;but not expressly provided for by such 
provisions (including, without limitation, the granting of unit appreciation 
rights, phantom unit rights or other rights with equity features), then the 
Board of Directors shall in good faith determine and implement an appropriate 
adjustment in the Conversion Price so as to protect the rights of such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder;<i> provided</i> that no such adjustment pursuant
to this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(iv)</u>&nbsp;will increase the Conversion Price 
as otherwise determined pursuant to this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)</u>;<i> provided
further</i> that if such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder does not accept such 
adjustments as appropriately protecting its interests hereunder against such 
dilution, then the Board of Directors and such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder 
shall agree, in good faith, upon an independent investment bank of nationally 
recognized standing to make such appropriate adjustments, whose determination 
shall be final and binding absent manifest error and whose fees and expenses 
shall be borne by the Partnership.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

size="1" style="font-

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Calculations</i>. The 
Partnership shall not issue fractional Units. If a distribution, subdivision, 
combination or conversion of Units would result in the issuance of fractional 
Units but for the provisions of <u>Section&nbsp;5.4(d)</u>&nbsp;and this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(h)</u>, each fractional Unit shall be rounded to the nearest
whole Unit.</p>

style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1

The Partnership may at any time any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units remain 
Outstanding, with the prior written consent of the Required Holders, reduce the 
then current Conversion Price to any amount and for any period of time deemed 
appropriate by the Board of Directors.</p>

THESE SECURITIES MAY&nbsp;NOT BE SOLD, OFFERED FOR SALE, PLEDGED, HYPOTHECATED 
OR OTHERWISE TRANSFERRED IN THE ABSENCE OF A REGISTRATION STATEMENT IN EFFECT 
WITH RESPECT TO THE SECURITIES UNDER SUCH ACT OR PURSUANT TO AN EXEMPTION FROM 
REGISTRATION THEREUNDER AND,&nbsp;IN THE CASE OF A TRANSACTION EXEMPT FROM 
REGISTRATION, UNLESS SOLD PURSUANT TO RULE 144 UNDER SUCH ACT OR THE ISSUER HAS 
RECEIVED DOCUMENTATION REASONABLY SATISFACTORY TO IT THAT SUCH TRANSACTION DOES
NOT REQUIRE REGISTRATION UNDER SUCH ACT.&#160; THIS SECURITY IS SUBJECT TO 
CERTAIN RESTRICTIONS ON TRANSFER SET FORTH IN (i)&nbsp;THE FIRST AMENDED AND 
RESTATED AGREEMENT OF LIMITED PARTNERSHIP OF THE PARTNERSHIP, DATED AS OF 
MAY&nbsp;14, 2013, AS AMENDED, AND (ii)&nbsp;THE SECURITIES PURCHASE AGREEMENT, 
DATED AS OF AUGUST 8, 2016, BY AND BETWEEN THE PARTNERSHIP AND THE SERIES A 
PURCHASER,&nbsp;IN EACH CASE, A COPY OF WHICH MAY&nbsp;BE OBTAINED FROM THE 
PARTNERSHIP AT ITS PRINCIPAL EXECUTIVE OFFICES.&#148;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(iii)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>In connection with a sale of 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units pursuant to an effective registration statement or
in reliance on Rule&nbsp;144 of the rules&nbsp;and regulations promulgated under
the Securities Act, upon receipt by the Partnership of such information as the 
Partnership reasonably deems necessary to determine that the sale of the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units is made in compliance with Rule&nbsp;144, the 
Partnership shall remove or cause to be removed the restrictive legend from the 
certificate(s)&nbsp;representing such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units (or the 
book-entry account maintained by the Transfer Agent), and the Partnership shall 
bear all costs associated therewith.</p>

size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(k)</font><font

size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Liquidation 
Preference</i>.&#160; In the event of any liquidation, dissolution and winding 
up of the Partnership under <u>Section&nbsp;12.4</u> or a sale, exchange or 
other disposition of all or substantially all of the assets of the Partnership, 
either voluntary or involuntary, the Record Holders of the Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units shall be entitled to receive, out of the assets of the 
Partnership available for distribution to the Partners or any assignees, prior 
and in preference to any distribution of any assets of the Partnership to the 
Record Holders of any other class or series of Partnership Interests, the 
positive value in each such holder&#146;s Capital Account in respect of such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units. If in the year of such liquidation and winding 
up, or sale, exchange or other disposition of all or substantially all of the 
assets of the Partnership, any such Record Holder&#146;s Capital Account in 
respect of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units is less than the aggregate 
Liquidation Preference of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units, then 
notwithstanding anything to the contrary contained in this Agreement, and prior 
to any other allocation pursuant to this Agreement for such year and prior to 
any distribution pursuant to the preceding sentence, items of gross income and 
gain shall be allocated to all Unitholders then holding Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Units, Pro Rata, until the Capital Account in respect of each Outstanding 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units is equal to the Liquidation Preference (and no
other allocation pursuant to this Agreement shall reverse the effect of such 
allocation). At the time of the dissolution of the Partnership, subject to 
Section&nbsp;17-804 of the Delaware Act, the Record Holders of the Series&nbsp;A
Preferred Units shall become entitled to receive any distributions in respect of
the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units that are accrued and unpaid as of the date of 
such distribution in priority over any entitlement of any other Partners or 
Assignees with respect to any distributions by the Partnership to such other 
Partners or Assignees; <i>provided, however</i>, that the General Partner, as 
such, will have no liability for any obligations with respect to such 
distributions to any Record Holder(s)&nbsp;of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units.</p>

whereupon the Partnership will forthwith issue and deliver upon the order of

Certificate (in accordance with <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(l)(iv)</u>, registered as 
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder may request, representing the outstanding 
number of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units being transferred by such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder and, if less than the entire outstanding number of 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units is being transferred, a new Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Unit Certificate (in accordance with <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(l)(iv)</u>) 
to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder representing the outstanding number of 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units not being transferred. Such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder and any assignee, by acceptance of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Unit Certificate, acknowledge and agree that, by reason of the provisions of 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)(ii)(B)</u>&nbsp;following conversion or redemption of any
of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units, the outstanding number of Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units represented by the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units may be less 
than the number of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units stated on the face of the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units.</p>

Certificates issued in connection with such issuance, does not exceed the number
of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units remaining outstanding under the original

new Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit Certificate), and (ii)&nbsp;shall have an

conversion and the like (and the computation thereof) shall be the amounts to be
received by a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder and shall not, except as expressly

obligations hereunder will cause irreparable harm to the Series&nbsp;A Preferred
Holders and that the remedy at law for any such breach may be inadequate. The 
Partnership therefore agrees that, in the event of any such breach or threatened
breach, each Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder shall be entitled, in addition to 
all other available remedies, to specific performance and/or temporary, 
preliminary and permanent injunctive or other equitable relief from any court of
competent jurisdiction in any such case without the necessity of proving actual 
damages and without posting a bond or other security. The Partnership shall 
provide all information and documentation to a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder 
that is requested by such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder to enable such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder to confirm the Partnership&#146;s compliance with

Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder (as the case may be) shall submit the dispute to 
the other party via facsimile or electronic mail (A)&nbsp;if by the Partnership,
within two (2)&nbsp;Business Days after the occurrence of the circumstances 
giving rise to such dispute or (B)&nbsp;if by such Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder at any time after such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder learned of the 
circumstances giving rise to such dispute.&#160; If such Series&nbsp;A Preferred
Holder and the Partnership are unable to promptly resolve such dispute relating 
to such Closing Bid Price, such Closing Sale Price, such Conversion Price, such 
Triggering Event Conversion Price, such VWAP or such fair market value, or the 
arithmetic calculation of such Conversion Rate or such applicable Redemption 
Price (as the case may be), at any time after the second (2nd) Business Day
following such initial notice by the Partnership or such Series&nbsp;A Preferred
Holder (as the case may be) of such dispute to the Partnership or such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder (as the case may be), then such Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder may, at its sole option, select an independent, reputable 
investment bank to resolve such dispute.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">documents referred to in the immediately preceding 
clauses (x)&nbsp;and (y)&nbsp;are collectively referred to herein as the 
&#147;<i>Required Dispute Documentation</i>&#148;) (it being understood and 
agreed that if either such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder or the Partnership 
fails to so deliver all of the Required Dispute Documentation by the Dispute 
Submission Deadline, then the party who fails to so submit all of the Required 
Dispute Documentation shall no longer be entitled to (and hereby waives its 
right to) deliver or submit any written documentation or other support to such 
investment bank with respect to such dispute and such investment bank shall 
resolve such dispute based solely on the Required Dispute Documentation that was
delivered to such investment bank prior to the Dispute Submission 
Deadline).&#160; Unless otherwise agreed to in writing by both the Partnership 
and such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder or otherwise requested by such 
investment bank, neither the Partnership nor such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder
shall be entitled to deliver or submit any written documentation or other 
support to such investment bank in connection with such dispute (other than the 
Required Dispute Documentation).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">C)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Partnership
and such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder shall cause such investment bank to 
determine the resolution of such dispute and notify the Partnership and such 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder of such resolution no later than ten
(10)&nbsp;Business Days immediately following the Dispute Submission Deadline. 
The fees and expenses of such investment bank shall be borne solely by the 
Partnership, and such investment bank&#146;s resolution of such dispute shall be
final and binding upon all parties absent manifest error.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(ii)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font><i>Miscellaneous</i>.&#160; The Partnership expressly acknowledges and 
agrees that (i)&nbsp;this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(p)</u>&nbsp;constitutes an 
agreement to arbitrate between the Partnership and each Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder (and constitutes an arbitration agreement) under &#167; 7501, et seq. of 
the New York Civil Practice Law and Rules&nbsp;(&#147;<i>CPLR</i>&#148;) and 
that any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder is authorized to apply for an order to 
compel arbitration pursuant to CPLR &#167; 7503(a)&nbsp;in order to compel 
compliance with this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(p)</u>, (ii)&nbsp;a dispute relating to
a Conversion Price includes, without limitation, disputes as to (A)&nbsp;whether
an issuance or sale or deemed issuance or sale of Common Units occurred under 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(i)</u>, (B)&nbsp;the consideration per Unit at which an 
issuance or deemed issuance of Common Units occurred, (C)&nbsp;whether any 
issuance or sale or deemed issuance or sale of Common Units was an issuance or 
sale or deemed issuance or sale of Excluded Securities, (D)&nbsp;whether an 
agreement, instrument, security or the like constitutes and Option or 
Convertible Security and (E)&nbsp;whether a Dilutive Issuance occurred, 
(iii)&nbsp;the terms of this Amendment and each other applicable Transaction 
Document shall serve as the basis for the selected investment bank&#146;s 
resolution of the applicable dispute, such investment bank shall be entitled 
(and is hereby expressly authorized) to make all findings, determinations and 
the like that such investment bank determines are required to be made by such 
investment bank in connection with its resolution of such dispute and in 
resolving such dispute such investment bank shall apply such findings, 
determinations and the like to the terms of this Amendment and any other 
applicable Transaction Documents, (iv)&nbsp;the applicable Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder (and only such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder with respect to 
disputes solely relating to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder), in its sole 
discretion, shall have the right to submit any dispute described in this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(p)</u>&nbsp;to any state or federal court sitting in The 
City of New York, Borough of Manhattan in lieu of utilizing the procedures set 
forth in this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(p)</u>&nbsp;and (v)&nbsp;nothing in this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(p)</u>&nbsp;shall limit such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder 
from obtaining</p>

Payments</i>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

size="1" style="font-

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font><i>Notices</i>.&#160; The Partnership shall provide each Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Holder with prompt written notice of all actions taken pursuant to the
terms of this Amendment, including in reasonable detail a description of such 
action and the reason therefor. Whenever notice is required to be given under 
this Amendment, unless otherwise provided herein, such notice must be in writing
and shall be given in accordance with <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(i)(v)</u>&nbsp;of the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase Agreement.&#160; The Partnership shall provide 
each Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder with prompt written notice of all actions 
taken pursuant to this Amendment, including in reasonable detail a description 
of such action and the reason therefore.&#160; Without limiting the generality 
of the foregoing, the Partnership shall give written notice to each 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder (i)&nbsp;immediately upon any adjustment of the 
Conversion Price, setting forth in reasonable detail, and certifying, the 
calculation of such adjustment and (ii)&nbsp;at least fifteen (15) days prior to
the date on which the Partnership closes its books or takes a record 
(A)&nbsp;with respect to any distribution upon the Common Units, (B)&nbsp;with 
respect to any grant, issuances, or sales of any Options, Convertible Securities
or rights to purchase Units, warrants, securities or other property to holders 
of Common Units or (C)&nbsp;for determining rights to vote with respect to any 
Fundamental Transaction, dissolution or liquidation;<i> provided</i> in each 
case that such information shall be made known to the public prior to or in 
conjunction with such notice being provided to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder. Upon receipt or delivery by the Partnership of any such notice or other 
notice required under this Amendment, unless the Partnership has in good faith 
determined that the matters relating to such notice do not constitute material, 
non-public information relating to the Partnership or any of its Subsidiaries, 
the Partnership shall within one (1)&nbsp;Business Day after any such receipt or
delivery publicly disclose such material, non-public information on a Current 
Report on Form&nbsp;8-K or otherwise. In the event that the Partnership believes
that such notice contains material, non-public information relating to the 
Partnership or any of its Subsidiaries, the Partnership so shall indicate to 
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder contemporaneously with delivery of such 
notice, and in the absence of any such indication, such Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Holder shall be allowed to presume that all matters relating to such notice do 
not constitute material, non-public information relating to the Partnership or 
any of its Subsidiaries. If the Partnership or any of its Subsidiaries provides 
material non-public information to a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder that is not 
publicly disclosed on a Current Report on Form&nbsp;8-K or otherwise within one 
(1)&nbsp;Business Day thereafter and such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder has not
agreed to receive such material non-public information, the Partnership hereby 
covenants and agrees that such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder shall not have any
duty of confidentiality to the Partnership, any of its Subsidiaries or any of 
their respective officers, directors, employees, affiliates or agents with 
respect to, or a duty to any of the foregoing not to trade on the basis of, such
material non-public information.&#160; Nothing contained in this 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(q)(i)</u>&nbsp;shall limit any obligations of the 
Partnership, or any rights of any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder, under the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase Agreement.</p>

are in United States Dollars (&#147;<i>U.S. Dollars</i>&#148;), and all amounts

denominated in other currencies (if any) shall be converted into the U.S. Dollar

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">Rate on the date of calculation. &#147;<i>Exchange 
Rate</i>&#148; means, in relation to any amount of currency to be converted into
U.S. Dollars pursuant to this Amendment, the U.S. Dollar exchange rate as 
published in the Wall Street Journal on the relevant date of calculation (it 
being understood and agreed that where an amount is calculated with reference 
to, or over, a period of time, the date of calculation shall be the final date 
of such period of time).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Payments</i>. Whenever any payment 
of cash is to be made by the Partnership to any Person pursuant to this 
Amendment, unless otherwise expressly set forth herein, such payment shall be 
made in lawful money of the United States of America by a certified check drawn 
on the account of the Partnership and sent via overnight courier service to such
Person at such address as previously provided to the Partnership in writing 
(which address, in the case of each of the Buyers (as defined in the 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase Agreement), shall initially be as set forth on 
the Schedule of Buyers attached to the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Purchase 
Agreement);<i> provided</i> that such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder may elect 
to receive a payment of cash via wire transfer of immediately available funds by
providing the Partnership with prior written notice setting out such request and
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder&#146;s wire transfer instructions. Whenever 
any amount expressed to be due by the terms of this Amendment is due on any day 
which is not a Business Day, the same shall instead be due on the next 
succeeding day which is a Business Day.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font><i>Judgment Currency</i>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

for the purpose of obtaining or enforcing judgment against the Partnership in 
any court in any jurisdiction it becomes necessary to convert into any other 
currency (such other currency being hereinafter in this Section&nbsp;24 referred
to as the &#147;<i>Judgment Currency</i>&#148;) an amount due in U.S. dollars 
under this Amendment, the conversion shall be made at the Exchange Rate 
prevailing on the Trading Day immediately preceding:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the date actual
payment of the amount due, in the case of any proceeding in the courts of New 
York or in the courts of any other jurisdiction that will give effect to such 
conversion being made on such date: or</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the date on 
which the foreign court determines, in the case of any proceeding in the courts 
of any other jurisdiction (the date as of which such conversion is made pursuant
to this <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(r)(i)(B)</u>&nbsp;being hereinafter referred to as 
the &#147;<i>Judgment Conversion Date</i>&#148;).</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

proceeding in the court of any jurisdiction referred to in 
<u>Section&nbsp;5.8(r)(i)(B)</u>&nbsp;above, there is a change in the Exchange 
Rate prevailing between the Judgment Conversion Date and the date of actual 
payment of the amount due, the applicable party shall pay such adjusted amount 
as may be necessary to ensure that the amount paid in the Judgment Currency, 
when converted at the Exchange Rate prevailing on the date of payment, will 
produce the amount of US dollars which could have been purchased with the amount
of Judgment Currency stipulated in the judgment or judicial order at the 
Exchange Rate prevailing on the Judgment Conversion Date.</p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:.5in;"><font

size="1" style="font-

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Any amount due from the Partnership 
under this provision shall be due as a separate debt and shall not be affected

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font

size="1" style="font-

#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font><i>Allocations</i>. Prior to the allocations set forth in 
<u>Section&nbsp;6.1(a)</u>, items of Partnership gross income shall be allocated
to the holders of the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units in amounts equal to the 
amount of cash actually distributed in respect of each such holder&#146;s 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units, until the aggregate amount of such items 
allocated pursuant hereto for the current taxable period and all previous 
taxable periods is equal to the cumulative amount of all cash distributions made
to the holders of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units pursuant to 
<u>Section&nbsp;6.3</u>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font>Section&nbsp;6.1(a)&nbsp;is hereby amended and restated as follows:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><i>Net Income and Net 
Loss</i>.&#160; After giving effect to the special allocations set forth in 
<u>Section&nbsp;6.1(b)</u>, Net Income and Net Loss for each taxable period and 
all items of income, gain, loss and deduction taken into account in computing 
Net Income and Net Loss for such taxable period shall be allocated to all 
Unitholders (other than holders of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units), Pro Rata.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font>Section&nbsp;6.1(b)(iii)&nbsp;is hereby amended and restated as
follows:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><i><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-
style:italic;">(iii)&nbsp;Priority Allocations</font></i>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If the amount 
of cash or the Net Agreed Value of any property distributed (except cash or 
property distributed pursuant to <u>Section&nbsp;12.4</u>) with respect to a 
Unit exceeds the amount of cash or the Net Agreed Value of property distributed 
with respect to another Unit, each Unitholder receiving such greater cash or 
property distribution shall be allocated gross income in an amount equal to the 
product of (A)&nbsp;the amount by which the distribution (on a per Unit basis) 
to such Unitholder exceeds the distribution with respect to the Unit receiving 
the smallest distribution and (B)&nbsp;the number of Units owned by the 
Unitholder receiving the greater distribution.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(B)&nbsp;With respect to any 
taxable period of the Partnership ending upon, or after, a Conversion Date, and 
after the application of <u>Section&nbsp;6.1(b)(iii)(A)</u>, all or a portion of
the remaining items of Partnership income, gain, loss or deduction for such 
taxable period shall be allocated 100% to each Partner holding a Common Unit 
converted from a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit until each such Partner has been 
allocated an amount of income, gain, loss and deduction that increases or 
decreases, as the case may be, the Capital Account maintained with respect to 
such Common Unit converted from a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit to equal, as 
closely as possible, the Per Unit Capital Amount for a then Outstanding Common 
Unit (other than a Common Unit converted from a Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Unit).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" 
face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(C)&nbsp;With respect to any 
taxable period of the Partnership ending upon, or after, the exercise of a 
Warrant, and after the application of <u>Sections 6.1(b)(iii)(A)&nbsp;and 
(B)</u>, all or a portion of the remaining items of Partnership income, gain, 
loss or deduction for such taxable period shall be allocated 100% to each 
Partner holding a Warrant Unit until each such Partner has been allocated an 
amount of income, gain, loss and deduction that increases or decreases, as the 
case may be, the Capital Account maintained with respect to such Warrant Unit to
equal, as closely as possible, the Per Unit Capital Amount for a then 
Outstanding Common Unit (other than a Warrant Unit).</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">40<a name="PB_40_072925_8146"></a></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font>Section&nbsp;6.2 is hereby amended to add a new subsection (g)&nbsp;as 
follows:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>If, as a result of an
exercise of a Noncompensatory Option, a Capital Account reallocation is required
under Treasury Regulation Section&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(2)(iv)(s)(3), the General 
Partner shall make corrective allocations pursuant to Treasury Regulation 
Section&nbsp;1.704-1(b)(4)(x).</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 
</font>Article&nbsp;VI is hereby amended to add a new Section&nbsp;6.4 as 
follows:</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times 
New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Section&nbsp;6.4&#160; <i>Special 
Provisions Relating to the Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holders</i>.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Except as otherwise 
provided in this Agreement, the holder of a Series&nbsp;A Preferred Unit shall 
have all of the rights and obligations of a Unitholder holding Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Units hereunder; <i>provided, however</i>, that as of the close of 
business on a Conversion Date, the rights of a holder of converted Series&nbsp;A
Preferred Units, in its capacity as such, shall cease with respect to such 
converted Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units and such holder (or such other Person to
whom Common Units are issued upon such conversion) shall possess all of the 
rights and obligations of a Unitholder holding Common Units hereunder, including
the right to vote as a holder of Common Units and the right to participate in 
allocations of income, gain, loss and deduction and distributions made with 
respect to Common Units; <i>provided, however</i>, that such converted 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units shall remain subject to the provisions of 
<u>Section&nbsp;6.1(b)(iii)(B)</u>&nbsp;and <u>Section&nbsp;6.4(b)</u>.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font 
size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font 
size="1" style="font-
size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&
#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#1
60;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>A Unitholder holding a 
Common Unit that has resulted from the conversion of a Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Unit pursuant to <u>Section&nbsp;5.8(b)</u>&nbsp;shall not be issued a Common 
Unit, and shall not be permitted to transfer such Common Unit to a Person that 
is not an Affiliate of the holder until such time as the General Partner 
determines, based on advice of counsel, that each such Common Unit should have, 
as a substantive matter, like intrinsic economic and federal income tax 
characteristics, in all material respects, to the intrinsic economic and federal
income tax characteristics of a Common Unit issued in the Initial 
Offering.&#160; In connection with the condition imposed by this 
<u>Section&nbsp;6.4(b)</u>, the General Partner shall use commercially 
reasonable efforts to take whatever steps are required to provide economic 
uniformity to such Common Units in preparation for a transfer of such Common 
Units, including the application of <u>Section&nbsp;6.1(b)(iii)(B)</u>; 
<i>provided</i>, <i>however</i>, that no such steps may be taken that would have
a material adverse effect on the Unitholders holding Common Units; <i>provided 
further</i> that if the General Partner is unable to provide economic uniformity
to such Common Units to be issued to any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder upon 
conversion of any Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units (each such applicable Common 
Unit, a &#147;<i>Series&nbsp;A Preferred Uniformity Failure Unit</i>,&#148; and 
each such event, a &#147;<i>Series A Preferred Uniformity Failure</i>&#148;) on 
or prior to the third (3rd) Trading Day after the Partnership&#146;s receipt of 
a Conversion Notice with respect thereto, in additional to all other rights and 
remedies of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder hereunder, (x)&nbsp;the 
Partnership shall deliver writing notice to such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder 
on or prior to such third (3<font size="1" style="font-
size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">rd</font>) Trading Day of the 
occurrence of such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Uniformity Failure, (y)&nbsp;all 
references to the term &#147;Triggering Event Conversion Price&#148; shall 
replace all references to the term &#147;Conversion Price&#148; for all purposes
hereunder with respect to such proposed conversion of Series&nbsp;A Preferred 
Units and each subsequent conversion of Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units hereunder 
and (z)&nbsp;if requested in writing by such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder, in 
lieu of delivering such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Uniformity Failure Units to such
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holder, such Conversion Notice shall be deemed null and 
void and such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units shall not be converted at such time 
hereunder.&#160; Within one (1)&nbsp;Trading Day after the Board of the General 
Partner determines that the Partnership is able to again issue and deliver to 
such Series&nbsp;A Preferred Holders, upon each subsequent conversion of 
Series&nbsp;A Preferred Units, Common Units that have, as a substantive matter, 
like intrinsic economic and federal income tax characteristics, in all material 
respects, to the intrinsic economic and federal income tax characteristics of a 
Common Unit issued in the Initial Offering (each, a &#147;<i>Series&nbsp;A 
Preferred Uniformity Cure Event</i>&#148;), the</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" 
style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-
align:center;">41<a name="PB_41_072323_8053"></a></p>

align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
